 1989 main aadhikarik rup se donon partiyon ke saath aane ke baad kai aise maukey aae jab bijepi or shivasena ke bich anban najar ai
 Shiv Sena founder Balasaheb Thackeray formed an alliance with the Bharatiya Janata Party in 1989
 bijepi kii taraf se swargeey pramod mahajan ne is gathbandhan main ahm bhoomika nibhaai

 jiske baad bijepi or shivasena ne milakar sarkaar banaai

" ’’ For any kind of recruitment in indo-tibetan Border Police (ITBP), the candidates will not have to go round the recruitment centers anymore
 iske liye itibipi ne samekit webportal laanch kiya he
 With the help of the first of its kind web portals in the Armed Forces, applications can be made for recruitment in Group d from Driver and Chef to Inspector and Doctor and Engineer
 itibipi ke mahanireekshak krishna choudhary ne haal hi main is webportal ko shuru karte huye is pahal ko sashastr balon ko paperles karne kii muhim se bhi joda
 Its specialty is that the interested candidate has to create only a profile on the portal
 profile main darj kii gai shaikshik yogyata ke mutabik portal se swat: use bataa diya jaayegaa ki vah itibipi main kin kin padon par bhartee ke yogya he
 After this, according to his eligibility, at the start of the application process, the candidate will be informed through email and mobile phone to join the recruitment
 itibipi ke pravaktaa vivek kumaar pandey ne bataaya ki sashastr balon main bhartee ke liye desh main pehali baar shuru hui is suvidha kii vajah se abhyarthiyon ko baar-baar vibhinn padon ke liye aavedan nahin karnaa padegaa
 This has not only increased the convenience of the candidates but also ensures transparency in the recruitment process, so that it can be avoided due to grievance complaints
 pandey ne ise ‘‘bhartee ke liye itibipi abhyarthi ke dwaara’’ seva bataate huye kaha ki rashtriya soochna kendra (enaisi) dwaara viksit is portal kaa payalat project pichley saal shuru kiya gaya tha
 It has now been started after making all the concrete arrangements to prevent the misuse of the data recorded in the portal
 portal par ek baar log in idi bana lene ke baad abhyarthi ko bhartee ke dauraan sirf chikitsa evam shaareerik pareekshan ke liye hi nikatatam bhartee centre par janaa padegaa
 The ITBP has connected its regional offices (frontier Zone) to this portal to connect interested candidates in remote areas with this service
 tippaniyan (apart from the headline, this news has not been edited by the NDTV team, it has been published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) ITBP spokesman Vivek Kumar Pandey said that due to this facility started for the first time in the country for recruitment in the Armed Forces, candidates will not have to repeatedly apply for various posts
 isse na sirf abhyarthiyon kii sahuuliyat badi he balki bhartee prakriya main paardarshita sunishchit hone se ise gadabadi kii shikayaton ke kaaran vilambit hone se bachaaya ja sakegaa
 Describing it as a "recruitment by ITBP candidates" service, Pandey said that the pilot project of this portal developed by the National Information Center (NIC) was started last year
 portal main darj data ke durupyog ko rokane ke liye sabhi pukhta intjaam karne ke baad ise ab shuru kiya gaya he
 Once the login ID is created on the portal, the candidate will have to go to the nearest recruitment center only for medical and physical examination during recruitment
